(function(apikey) {
var boomr_url = "https://s.go-mpulse.net/boomerang/" + apikey,
where = document.currentScript || document.getElementById("boomerang-loader-script"),
promoted = false,
LOADER_TIMEOUT = 3000;
function promote() {
var s;
s = document.createElement("script");
s.id = "boomr-scr-as";
s.src = this.href;
// not really needed since dynamic scripts are async by default and the script is already in cache at this point,
// but some naive parsers will see a missing async attribute and think we're not async
s.async = true;
where.parentNode.appendChild(s);
window.BOOMR_API_key = apikey;
promoted = true;
}
function iframe_loader() {
promoted = true;
// Boomerang Loader Snippet version 10
if (window.BOOMR && (window.BOOMR.version || window.BOOMR.snippetExecuted)) {
return;
}

var dom, doc, iframe = document.createElement("iframe"), win = window;
function boomerangSaveLoadTime(e) {
win.BOOMR_onload = (e && e.timeStamp) || new Date().getTime();
}
if (win.addEventListener) {
win.addEventListener("load", boomerangSaveLoadTime, false);
} else if (win.attachEvent) {
win.attachEvent("onload", boomerangSaveLoadTime);
}

iframe.title = "";
iframe.role = "presentation";
(iframe.frameElement || iframe).style.cssText = "width:0;height:0;border:0;display:none;";

}

};

win.addEventListener("load", win._boomrl, false);
} else if (win.attachEvent) {
win.attachEvent("onload", win._boomrl);
}
win.document.close();
}
var l = document.createElement("link");
if (l.relList && typeof l.relList.supports === "function" && l.relList.supports("preload") && ("as" in l)) {

l.rel = "preload";

l.addEventListener("error", iframe_loader);

}
}, LOADER_TIMEOUT);

  <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
    <a itemprop="url" href="/news/article-6843285/Trump-plays-golf-Kid-Rock-Mar-Lago-speculation-mounts-Mueller-Reports-findings.html">Tight-lipped Trump plays golf with Kid Rock in Florida while AG Barr returns home from a day scouring Mueller's report at his DC office, but keeps the world waiting for his findings&nbsp;</a>
  </h2>
  <a href="/news/article-6843285/Trump-plays-golf-Kid-Rock-Mar-Lago-speculation-mounts-Mueller-Reports-findings.html">
    <img data-mol-fe-video-preview="" src="https://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2019/03/24/408320733870309920/964x580_JPG-SINGLE_408320733870309920.jpg" width="964" height="508" data-video="https://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2019/03/24/408320733870309920/964x580_MP4_408320733870309920.mp4" data-film="https://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2019/03/24/408320733870309920/308x174_JPG_408320733870309920.jpg" data-frame-width="308" data-frame-height="162" data-frame-count="45" data-fps="7" data-hd-film="https://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2019/03/24/408320733870309920/636x382_JPG-HD_408320733870309920.jpg" data-hd-frame-width="636" data-hd-frame-height="336" data-hd-frame-count="45" data-hd-fps="7" class=" b-loaded"><video loop="" style="height: 508px; width: 964px; display: none;"><source src="https://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2019/03/24/408320733870309920/964x580_MP4_408320733870309920.mp4" type="video/mp4"></video>
<noscript>
    <img src="https://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2019/03/24/408320733870309920/964x580_JPG-SINGLE_408320733870309920.jpg" width="964" height=508 />
</noscript>

  </a>
  <div class="articletext">
    <div>
      <p>
        
        President Trump was photographed smiling next to Kid Rock (left), the Bawitdaba crooner, at his Trump International Golf Club in West Palm Beach on Saturday. Kid Rock, who posted the image on his Twitter account, was appropriately dressed for the occasion. He wore a red sweater vest over a white collared shirt, which complemented his American-flag style slacks and what looked like a gold belt. Trump has spent the day at his Florida golf course (inset), while his attorney general, William Barr (right), was at the Justice Department reading the Mueller Report before arriving home later in the evening.Speculation suggests that Barr will brief Congress on his key findings on Sunday. Lawmakers are now bracing for the aftermath, even though the contents of the long-awaited report are still being kept secret.&nbsp;
      </p>
    </div>

                          <div itemscope="" itemtype="//schema.org/ListItem" itemprop="itemListElement" class="article article-large cleared" data-original-title="Barbra Streisand says Michael Jacksons accuser's parents 'were seduced by fame'">
  <meta itemprop="position" content="2">
  <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
    <a itemprop="url" href="/news/article-6842751/Barbra-Streisand-says-Michael-Jacksons-accusers-parents-seduced-fame.html">'The parents were seduced by fame': Barbra Streisand apologizes for defending friend Michael Jackson, but STILL blames his two accusers' parents because their most important role was 'protecting their children'&nbsp;</a>
  </h2>
  <a href="/news/article-6842751/Barbra-Streisand-says-Michael-Jacksons-accusers-parents-seduced-fame.html">
        <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/23/20/11370464-0-image-m-10_1553373803886.jpg" height="500" width="308" alt="Barbra Streisand says Michael Jacksons accuser's parents 'were seduced by fame'">
    
      <noscript>
    
        <img  src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/23/20/11370464-0-image-m-10_1553373803886.jpg" height="500" width="308" alt="Barbra Streisand says Michael Jacksons accuser's parents 'were seduced by fame'" />
    
      </noscript>
  </a>
  <div class="articletext-holder">
    <p>
      
      Barbra Streisand, 76, said she 'feels nothing but sympathy for the men' after she was forced to respond to her earlier comments. But Streisand said of Stephanie Safechuck, top right inset, and Joy Robson, bottom right inset, that 'its clear that the parents of the two young men were also victimized and seduced by fame and fantasy'. Streisand had said the alleged sexual abuse victims 'wanted to be there' as kids. She was referring to now-adults Wade Robson and James Safechuck. The two men are the subjects of recent documentary, 'Leaving Neverland,' which details their alleged sexual abuse at the hands of Jackson, from ages seven and 10. Streisand told British newspaper The Times that she believes their allegations, but it 'didn't kill them' and Jackson's 'sexual needs were his sexual needs'.
    </p>

  </h2>

    <p>

                <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/24/00/11375394-0-image-a-11_1553385767030.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Democrats debate Mueller strategy as findings loom">
            
              <noscript>
            
                <img  src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/24/00/11375394-0-image-a-11_1553385767030.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Democrats debate Mueller strategy as findings loom" />
            
              </noscript>
        </a>
        <div>
        <p>
            
            'Once we get the principal conclusions of the report, I think it's entirely possible that [it] will be a good day for the president and his core supporters,' Senator Chris Coons (right) of Delaware said on Saturday. Congressional Democrats plotted strategy Saturday as they awaited the conclusions of Robert Mueller's (inset) Russia investigation, with senior lawmakers demanding full transparency and preparing for next steps if the results were favorable to President Trump (left). House Democrats conferenced by phone to share what they knew about the probe and to discuss how to move forward.
        </p>

  <div class="articletext">
    <div>
     <p>
       
       On Saturday police announced they have arrested the man behind the brutal assault of a 78-year-old woman riding the New York subway on March 10. The unidentified man was caught on tape repeatedly punching and kicking the woman in the face and body as they rode the northbound 2 train in the Bronx at 3.10am. Police posted his image on Twitter on Friday night for tips on his identity. By Saturday they arrested him. NYPD Chief Dermot F. Shea announced the arrest and said the victim was treated for her injuries and released from a hospital and is 'getting the care, advocacy and support needed'.

    </h2>
    <div class="articletext">
        <a href="/news/article-6843083/The-beguiling-beauty-reportedly-shut-Royals-Norfolk-circle-Kates-orders.html">

        <p>
            
            Described most frequently as a beguiling socialite, the willowy Rose Hanbury (left with William and Kate), Marchioness of Cholmondeley, has always commanded attention. As a renowned society beauty and former model with an impeccably aristocratic pedigree, there were no shortage of suitors for her hand including, it was once rumoured, a young Prince William. The honour eventually fell to charismatic David Rocksavage, the 7th Marquess of Cholmondeley  a wealthy Old Etonian 23 years her senior  with whom she now has three children. Rose has always liked to defy convention, according to friends. The tall, leggy and doe-eyed brunette, now 35, signed up to model agency Storm, the firm that was also home to Kate Moss, when she arrived on the London scene with elder sister Marina. The sisters came to public attention in 2005 after the publication of a racy photograph (right) showing them in matching skimpy pink bikinis flanking then-Prime Minister Tony Blair.

    <img data-mol-fe-video-preview="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="https://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2019/03/23/6833791010805401454/636x382_JPG-SINGLE_6833791010805401454.jpg" width="636" height="380" data-video="https://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2019/03/23/6833791010805401454/636x382_MP4_6833791010805401454.mp4" data-film="https://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2019/03/23/6833791010805401454/308x174_JPG_6833791010805401454.jpg" data-frame-width="308" data-frame-height="184" data-frame-count="46" data-fps="7" data-hd-film="https://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2019/03/23/6833791010805401454/636x382_JPG-HD_6833791010805401454.jpg" data-hd-frame-width="636" data-hd-frame-height="380" data-hd-frame-count="46" data-hd-fps="7">

  <div class="articletext">
    <div>
     <p>
       
       A faulty escalator at the main railway station for Disneyland Paris sparked mass panic (pictured) on Saturday night as families could be seen shrieking and rushing away from the resort. There were fears of explosions and even gunshots, but a spokesman for the RER station at Marne la Vallee said: 'It seems that a malfunctioning escalator has caused the problems.' Police and soldiers were seen flooding the area around the station, which is around 20 miles from the centre of the French capital. It follows warnings from terrorist groups including Islamic State and Al-Qaeda that Disneyland is a prime target.

     <p>
       
       A cruise ship has issued a mayday call after suffering engine failure in high winds off the coast of Norway. Rescue helicopters have been airlifting the 1,300 passengers from the ship called Viking Sky. The ship, built in 2017, belongs to Viking Ocean Cruises founded by Norwegian billionaire Torstein Hagen. Winds reached a speed of 38 knots at the time of the incident.
     </p>

    <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
        <a itemprop="url" href="/femail/article-6843297/Why-80-year-old-great-grandmother-spent-10-000-risked-life-face-lift.html">'The doctor warned me I could die, but I told him "at least I'll look good in my coffin"': Why this 80-year-old great-grandmother spent $13,000 - and risked her life for a face lift</a>
    </h2>
    <div class="articletext">
        <a href="/femail/article-6843297/Why-80-year-old-great-grandmother-spent-10-000-risked-life-face-lift.html">
                <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/23/22/11373520-0-image-a-63_1553381303048.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Why this 80-year-old great-grandmother spent 10,000 - and risked her life for a face lift">
            
              <noscript>
            
                <img  src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/23/22/11373520-0-image-a-63_1553381303048.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Why this 80-year-old great-grandmother spent 10,000 - and risked her life for a face lift" />
            
              </noscript>
        </a>
        <div>
        <p>
            
            It was only when, strip by strip, the bandages were peeled away that Toni Goldenberg, from the UK, finally knew for sure. Tentatively, she touched her neck. Then, as a mirror was held up to her newly exposed face, she gasped in delight. A miracle was staring back. At the remarkable age of 80, the great grandmother had just undergone a three-and-a-half-hour facelift, knowing that she risked dangerous complications  or even death  under the surgeons knife. Toni had spent years scrimping and saving from her meagre pension for the 10,000 operation, driven to fulfil a long-held dream. And now, with her daughter at her side, she knew for certain that the loathed lines, wrinkles and crepe skin had finally been smoothed away. The biggest gamble of her life had paid off. They told me there were risks, but I was determined, she explains today. I said to the doctor, If I die, I die.
        </p>

          <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/23/02/11349930-0-image-a-46_1553309770720.jpg" height="115" width="154" alt="">

    <img src="https://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2019/03/23/580617390487879268/636x382_JPG-SINGLE_580617390487879268.jpg" width="636" height=382 />
</noscript>

  </a>
  <div class="articletext">
    <div>
     <p>
       
       A Verizon worker was suspended from his job for rescuing a cat which was stranded on top of a telephone pole.Maurice German was working in a neighborhood in Port Richmond, Pennsylvania last Saturday, when a resident asked him to help rescue 'Momma' the cat. The feline had been stuck on top of the pole for about 12 hours, CBS Philly reported.German obliged by using a boom lift to reach the cat as residents filmed the rescue operation and applauded the man. The cat was safely returned to its owner and was not harmed.But Verizon suspended German for 15 days, saying its vehicles and equipment were not intended to be used in the area where he operated.Verizon spokesperson Rich Young told CBS Philly: 'We take no joy in this job action.'However, were committed and responsible for keeping our employees and customers safe while working in a particular area.'
     </p>

                <div itemscope="" itemtype="//schema.org/ListItem" itemprop="itemListElement" class="article article-tri-headline">
    <meta itemprop="position" content="61">
    <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
        <a itemprop="url" href="/news/article-6842297/Terminally-ill-British-mother-40-shocks-medics-tumour-shrinks-75.html">Terminally-ill mother, 40, who kept her lung cancer secret from her young daughter shocks medics after tumor shrinks by 75% following alternative treatment in Mexico&nbsp;</a>
    </h2>
    <div class="articletext">
        <a href="/news/article-6842297/Terminally-ill-British-mother-40-shocks-medics-tumour-shrinks-75.html">
                <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/23/15/11364062-0-image-a-16_1553355836114.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Terminally-ill British mother, 40, shocks medics after tumour shrinks by 75%">
            
              <noscript>
            
                <img  src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/23/15/11364062-0-image-a-16_1553355836114.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Terminally-ill British mother, 40, shocks medics after tumour shrinks by 75%" />
            
              </noscript>
        </a>
        <div>
        <p>
            
            Kate Malvenan, 40, was given the cancer diagnosis in October last year where doctors told her she only had months left to live. After a friend told her about a clinic in Mexico which offered alternative cancer treatments, she remortgaged her house to fund the 35,000 programme. Once she finished the three-week stint at the centre, she went back home to Queensland, Australia, where her new x-rays shocked doctors by showing her tumour had shrunk by 75 per cent.
        </p>
    </div>

                <div itemscope="" itemtype="//schema.org/ListItem" itemprop="itemListElement" class="article article-tri-headline">
    <meta itemprop="position" content="62">
    <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
        <a itemprop="url" href="/news/article-6842417/Double-amputee-rescued-island-middle-Rio-Grande-River.html">Legless man is rescued from an island in the middle of the Rio Grande River trying to cross into the U.S.&nbsp;</a>
    </h2>
    <div class="articletext">
        <a href="/news/article-6842417/Double-amputee-rescued-island-middle-Rio-Grande-River.html">
                <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/23/16/11364684-0-image-a-5_1553357708229.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Double-amputee is rescued from an island in the middle of the Rio Grande River">
            
              <noscript>
            
                <img  src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/23/16/11364684-0-image-a-5_1553357708229.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Double-amputee is rescued from an island in the middle of the Rio Grande River" />
            
              </noscript>
        </a>
        <div>
        <p>
            
            A double-amputee was rescued from an island in the middle of the Rio Grande River this week while trying to make his way into the United States. Agents from the Eagle Pass Station marine unit said they saw the vulnerable 37-year-old man by himself in a wheelchair stranded on an island in the center of the river. The Border Patrol says he was determined to be in the United States illegally and was assisted to the U.S. shore for medical attention and processing.
        </p>
    </div>
</div>

     <p>
       
       A North Carolina woman has sued the owner of a Subway outlet after he allegedly slapped her during a dispute over a sandwich.Elizabeth Hinson, who goes by the name Tina Richardson, went to a Subway franchise by Kenneth Lancaster in Concord on March 8 to get a Sesame-Ginger Glazed Chicken Wrap for an elderly woman.However he later slapped her in the face during an argument after she asked for a refund, according to a lawsuit seen by ABC News.The elderly lady told Richardson the wrap did not resemble the picture on the flyer advertisement and did not have a taste of ginger. She subsequent returned to the Subway to request a refund, which the employee refused, according to the complaint.Lancaster then appeared from the back and yelled expletives at her and told her to leave the store.Richardson later shared footage of the incident on her Facebook page, which shows Lancaster walking towards her aggressively and raising his hand up.

                <div itemscope="" itemtype="//schema.org/ListItem" itemprop="itemListElement" class="article article-tri-headline">
    <meta itemprop="position" content="77">
    <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
        <a itemprop="url" href="/news/article-6842847/Northern-lights-appear-New-York-states-weekend.html">Northern lights could appear over New York and other states this weekend as a geomagnetic storm is expected to strike on Saturday night</a>
    </h2>
    <div class="articletext">
        <a href="/news/article-6842847/Northern-lights-appear-New-York-states-weekend.html">
                <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/23/20/11370478-0-image-a-32_1553374142532.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Northern lights could appear over New York and other US states this weekend">
            
              <noscript>
            
                <img  src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/23/20/11370478-0-image-a-32_1553374142532.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Northern lights could appear over New York and other US states this weekend" />
            
              </noscript>
        </a>
        <div>
        <p>
            
            New Yorkers and a handful of other Americans may not have to travel to the remote glaciers of Greenland or Iceland to catch a glimpse of one of the world's most fascinating phenomenons this weekend - it may be coming to them instead. According to the National Oceanic and Atmospheric Administration (NOAA), a geomagnetic storm may make the Aurora Borealis visible over Upstate New York this weekend, and may even extend to other parts of Northern America. Such regions are projected include New Hampshire, Vermont, Maine, Michigan, Wisconsin, Minnesota, North and South Dakota, Montana, Northern Idaho and Washington state.
        </p>
    </div>
</div>

                <div itemscope="" itemtype="//schema.org/ListItem" itemprop="itemListElement" class="article article-tri-headline">
    <meta itemprop="position" content="83">
    <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
        <a itemprop="url" href="/news/article-6842949/Giant-cocktail-shaker-serving-2-400-gallons-alcohol-goes-tour-Florida.html">Giant cocktail shaker serving 2,400 gallons of alcohol from a cement mix style truck goes on a tour of Florida</a>
    </h2>
    <div class="articletext">
        <a href="/news/article-6842949/Giant-cocktail-shaker-serving-2-400-gallons-alcohol-goes-tour-Florida.html">
                <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/23/20/11370666-0-image-a-93_1553374468516.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Giant cocktail shaker serving 2,400 gallons of alcohol goes on a tour of Florida">
            
              <noscript>
            
                <img  src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/23/20/11370666-0-image-a-93_1553374468516.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Giant cocktail shaker serving 2,400 gallons of alcohol goes on a tour of Florida" />
            
              </noscript>
        </a>
        <div>
        <p>
            
            The&nbsp;27-feet long, 13 feet tall shaker can hold 2,400 gallons of alcohol. That is the equivalent of 123,000 bottles of Monkey Shoulder, makers say. Its filled with whiskey, mint simple syrup, fresh lemon juice, soda and mint. The truck will head to various locations around&nbsp;Orlando next week. It comes complete with rotating drum to mix the&nbsp;Mixed Up Monkey cocktail.
        </p>
    </div>
</div>

    </h2>
    <div class="articletext">
        <a href="/news/article-6842173/Shaolin-Monkeys-Pair-raging-primates-come-blows-brutal-Kung-Fu-showdown.html">
                <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/23/15/11361134-0-image-a-133_1553353511747.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Shaolin Monkeys! Pair of raging primates come to blows in brutal Kung Fu showdown">
            
              <noscript>
            
                <img  src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/23/15/11361134-0-image-a-133_1553353511747.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Shaolin Monkeys! Pair of raging primates come to blows in brutal Kung Fu showdown" />
            
              </noscript>
        </a>
        <div>
        <p>
            
            Wildlife photographer Sergey Savvi snapped the pair as they landed martial arts-style flying kicks at Kaeng Krachen National Park in Phetchaburi, Thailand, as they tried to assert dominance. Mr Savvi said, from Saint Petersburg, Russia, said: 'I have never seen anything like this before. Dusky leaf monkeys spend the most of their time feeding or resting up trees, so to see them on the ground is very rare.'
        </p>
    </div>
</div>

                <div class="article article-tri-headline">
  <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
    <a href="/news/article-6841843/Over-friendly-lion-mistakes-4x4-one-pride-starts-licking-nuzzling-vehicle.html">ROAR emotion! Friendly lion mistakes 4x4 for one of his own pride and starts licking and nuzzling vehicle in South African wilderness</a>
  </h2>
  <a href="/news/article-6841843/Over-friendly-lion-mistakes-4x4-one-pride-starts-licking-nuzzling-vehicle.html">
    <img data-mol-fe-video-preview="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="https://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2019/03/23/5626058878391140119/636x382_JPG-SINGLE_5626058878391140119.jpg" width="636" height="382" data-video="https://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2019/03/23/5626058878391140119/636x382_MP4_5626058878391140119.mp4" data-film="https://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2019/03/23/5626058878391140119/308x174_JPG_5626058878391140119.jpg" data-frame-width="308" data-frame-height="184" data-frame-count="58" data-fps="7" data-hd-film="https://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2019/03/23/5626058878391140119/636x382_JPG-HD_5626058878391140119.jpg" data-hd-frame-width="636" data-hd-frame-height="382" data-hd-frame-count="58" data-hd-fps="7">
<noscript>
    <img src="https://video.dailymail.co.uk/preview/mol/2019/03/23/5626058878391140119/636x382_JPG-SINGLE_5626058878391140119.jpg" width="636" height=382 />
</noscript>

  </a>
  <div class="articletext">
    <div>
     <p>
       
       Shane the 15-year-old African lion shows his affection to large cars that pass by. He is seen grooming, rubbing and licking them as though they are other lions that he has to look after. The conservation director at GG Conservation, Suzanne Scott, 50, said it was surprising to see the unusual behaviour but it makes her feel like 'part of his pride'. Shane, from Harrismith, South Africa, cosies up to big cars as they drive through the reserve he lives on. African lions are considered the most social of all the big cats and usually live in prides containing 10-15 others.
     </p>
    </div>
  </div>

                <div itemscope="" itemtype="//schema.org/ListItem" itemprop="itemListElement" class="article article-tri-headline">
    <meta itemprop="position" content="90">
    <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
        <a itemprop="url" href="/femail/article-6810881/New-Zealand-couple-offer-Airbnb-guests-chance-stay-Beatles-esque-submarine.html">'Mad scientist' builds a SUBMARINE from scratch in the forest - and has been stunned by the array of people eager to spend the night inside</a>
    </h2>
    <div class="articletext">
        <a href="/femail/article-6810881/New-Zealand-couple-offer-Airbnb-guests-chance-stay-Beatles-esque-submarine.html">
                <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/15/06/11020996-0-image-a-107_1552629623099.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="New Zealand couple offer Airbnb guests the chance to stay in Beatles-esque submarine">
            
              <noscript>
            
                <img  src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/15/06/11020996-0-image-a-107_1552629623099.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="New Zealand couple offer Airbnb guests the chance to stay in Beatles-esque submarine" />
            
              </noscript>
        </a>
        <div>
        <p>
            
            A self-confessed 'mad scientist' from New Zealand who hand-crafted a yellow submarine (left, top and bottom right) is offering Airbnb guests the experience of a lifetime - and all for $130 a night. Keith Lovelock (inset) built the submarine from scratch using a range of recycled items and bits he had lying around his shed. 'We thought it was going to be our playhouse, but it's just taken on a life of its own. I was called a daydreamer at school,' he told FEMAIL.
        </p>
    </div>
</div>

  </h2>
  <div class="articletext">
    <a href="/news/article-6838539/Botswana-baby-buffalo-comes-seconds-eaten-lion.html">
          <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/22/10/11316696-0-image-a-38_1553250552587.jpg" height="115" width="154" alt="">
      
        <noscript>
      
          <img  src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/22/10/11316696-0-image-a-38_1553250552587.jpg" height="115" width="154" alt="" />
      
        </noscript>
    </a>
    <p>
        
        Veterinary surgeon Ben Cranke, 54, captured these incredible images of the battle between the big cat and a herd of buffalo in Botswana in southern Africa.

  <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
    <a itemprop="url" href="/news/article-6838181/Light-beam-appears-travel-steps-escalator-like-slinky-toy-spooky-illusion.html">Trick of the light! Beam appears to travel down the steps of an escalator like a slinky toy in spooky illusion</a>
  </h2>
  <div class="articletext">
    <a href="/news/article-6838181/Light-beam-appears-travel-steps-escalator-like-slinky-toy-spooky-illusion.html">
          <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/22/09/11314100-0-image-m-2_1553246599852.jpg" height="115" width="154" alt="">
      
        <noscript>

        </noscript>
    </a>
    <p>
        
        The beam of light was spotted on an office building escalator during a sunny morning in Toronto, Canada. As the steps move upwards, the light appears to jump from step to step.

                <div itemscope="" itemtype="//schema.org/ListItem" itemprop="itemListElement" class="article article-tri-headline">
    <meta itemprop="position" content="93">
    <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
        <a itemprop="url" href="/news/article-6842123/Central-Parks-resident-Mandarin-duck-faces-competition-stunning-Great-Blue-Heron.html">Central Park's resident Mandarin duck faces competition from stunning Great Blue Heron after rare sighting in one of its ponds</a>
    </h2>
    <div class="articletext">
        <a href="/news/article-6842123/Central-Parks-resident-Mandarin-duck-faces-competition-stunning-Great-Blue-Heron.html">
                <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/23/13/11360080-0-image-a-4_1553346191367.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Central Park's resident Mandarin duck faces competition from stunning Great Blue Heron">
            
              <noscript>
            
                <img  src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/1s/2019/03/23/13/11360080-0-image-a-4_1553346191367.jpg" height="382" width="636" alt="Central Park's resident Mandarin duck faces competition from stunning Great Blue Heron" />
            
              </noscript>
        </a>
        <div>
        <p>
            
            A Great Blue Heron has become the latest bird to steal the limelight from Central Park's well-known wildlife residents.A picture of the majestic bird, which is electric blue in color, was shared on Twitter last week by photographer Rosalie Quinto-Domingo.She spotted the Great Blue Heron at The Pond, which is also home to the Mandarin duck.She said: 'I just came out from work nearby late afternoon and decided to drop by the Pond and then there's this beautiful Great Blue Heron standing on the dead tree and I quickly grab my camera to take a few shots.'The Great Blue Heron has its origins in South East Asia. But David Barrett, who manages the Manhattan Bird Alert Twitter account that keeps followers abreast of the latest rare bird sightings and beyond, claimed that Great Blue Herons can be seen throughout the year.
        </p>
    </div>
</div>
